17 package org.http4s.ember.core.h2
18 
19 import cats._
20 import cats.data._
21 import cats.effect._
22 import cats.syntax.all._
23 import fs2._
24 import org.typelevel.log4cats.Logger
25 import scodec.bits._

27 import java.util.concurrent.CancellationException
28 import scala.annotation.nowarn

30 // Will eventually hold client/server through single interface matching that of the designed paradigm
31 // in StreamState
32 @nowarn("msg=implicit numeric widening")
33 private[h2] class H2Stream[F[_]: Concurrent](
34     val id: Int,
35     localSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings,
36     connectionType: H2Connection.ConnectionType,
37     val remoteSettings: F[H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings],
38     val state: Ref[F, H2Stream.State[F]],
39     val hpack: Hpack[F],
40     val enqueue: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Chunk[H2Frame]],
41     val onClosed: F[Unit],
42     val goAway: H2Error => F[Unit],
43     private[this] val logger: Logger[F],
44 ) {
45   import H2Stream.StreamState
46 
47   def sendPushPromise(originating: Int, headers: NonEmptyList[(String, String, Boolean)]): F[Unit] =
48     connectionType match {
49       case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server =>
50         state.get.flatMap { s =>
51           s.state match {
52             case StreamState.Idle =>
53               for {
54                 h <- hpack.encodeHeaders(headers)
55                 frame = H2Frame.PushPromise(originating, true, id, h, None)
56                 _ <- state.update(s => s.copy(state = StreamState.ReservedLocal))
57                 _ <- enqueue.offer(Chunk.singleton(frame))
58               } yield ()
59             case _ =>
60               new IllegalStateException(
61                 "Push Promises are only allowed on an idle Stream"
62               ).raiseError
63           }
64         }
65       case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client =>
66         new IllegalStateException("Clients Are Not Allowed To Send PushPromises").raiseError
67     }
68 
69   // TODO Check Settings to Split Headers into Headers and Continuation
70   def sendHeaders(headers: NonEmptyList[(String, String, Boolean)], endStream: Boolean): F[Unit] =
71     state.get.flatMap { s =>
72       s.state match {
73         case StreamState.Idle | StreamState.HalfClosedRemote | StreamState.Open |
74             StreamState.ReservedLocal =>
75           hpack
76             .encodeHeaders(headers)
77             .map(bv => H2Frame.Headers(id, None, endStream, true, bv, None))
78             .flatMap(f => enqueue.offer(Chunk.singleton(f))) <*
79             state
80               .modify { b =>
81                 val newState: StreamState = (b.state, endStream) match {
82                   case (StreamState.Idle, false) => StreamState.Open
83                   case (StreamState.Idle, true) => StreamState.HalfClosedLocal
84                   case (StreamState.HalfClosedRemote, false) => StreamState.HalfClosedRemote
85                   case (StreamState.HalfClosedRemote, true) => StreamState.Closed
86                   case (StreamState.Open, false) => StreamState.Open
87                   case (StreamState.Open, true) => StreamState.HalfClosedLocal
88                   case (StreamState.ReservedLocal, true) => StreamState.Closed
89                   case (StreamState.ReservedLocal, false) => StreamState.HalfClosedRemote
90                   case (s, _) => s // Hopefully Impossible
91                 }
92                 (b.copy(state = newState), newState)
93               }
94               .flatMap { state =>
95                 if (state == StreamState.Closed) onClosed else Applicative[F].unit
96               }
97               .void
98         case _ => new IllegalStateException("Stream Was Closed").raiseError
99       }
100     }
101 
102   def sendData(bv: ByteVector, endStream: Boolean): F[Unit] = state.get.flatMap { s =>
103     s.state match {
104       case StreamState.Open | StreamState.HalfClosedRemote =>
105         if (bv.size.toInt <= s.writeWindow && s.writeWindow > 0) {
106           enqueue.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Data(id, bv, None, endStream))) >> {
107             state
108               .modify { s =>
109                 val newState = if (endStream) {
110                   s.state match {
111                     case StreamState.Open => StreamState.HalfClosedLocal
112                     case StreamState.HalfClosedRemote => StreamState.Closed
113                     case state => state // Ruh-roh
114                   }
115                 } else s.state
116                 (
117                   s.copy(
118                     state = newState,
119                     writeWindow = s.writeWindow - bv.size.toInt,
120                   ),
121                   newState,
122                 )
123               }
124               .flatMap(state => if (state == StreamState.Closed) onClosed else Applicative[F].unit)
125           }
126         } else {
127           if (s.writeWindow > 0) {
128             for {
129               t <- state.modify { s =>
130                 val head = bv.take(s.writeWindow)
131                 val tail = bv.drop(s.writeWindow)
132                 (s.copy(writeWindow = s.writeWindow - head.size.toInt), (head, tail))
133               }
134               (head, tail) = t
135               _ <- enqueue.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Data(id, head, None, false)))
136               out <- sendData(tail, endStream)
137             } yield out
138 
139           } else s.writeBlock.get.rethrow >> sendData(bv, endStream)
140         }
141       case _ => new IllegalStateException("Stream Was Closed").raiseError
142     }
143   }
144 
145   def receiveHeaders(headers: H2Frame.Headers, continuations: H2Frame.Continuation*): F[Unit] =
146     state.get.flatMap { s =>
147       s.state match {
148         case StreamState.Open | StreamState.HalfClosedLocal | StreamState.Idle |
149             StreamState.ReservedRemote =>
150           val block = headers.headerBlock ++ continuations.foldLeft(ByteVector.empty) {
151             case (acc, cont) => acc ++ cont.headerBlockFragment
152           }
153           for {
154             h <- hpack.decodeHeaders(block).onError { case e =>
155               logger.error(e)(s"Issue in headers") >> goAway(H2Error.CompressionError)
156             }
157             newstate =
158               if (headers.endStream) s.state match {
159                 case StreamState.Open => StreamState.HalfClosedRemote // Client
160                 case StreamState.Idle => StreamState.HalfClosedRemote // Server
161                 case StreamState.HalfClosedLocal => StreamState.Closed // Client
162                 case StreamState.ReservedRemote => StreamState.Closed
163                 case s => s
164               }
165               else
166                 s.state match {
167                   case StreamState.Idle => StreamState.Open // Server
168                   case StreamState.ReservedRemote => StreamState.HalfClosedLocal
169                   case s => s
170                 }
171             t <- state.modify(s => (s.copy(state = newstate), (s.request, s.response)))
172             (request, response) = t
173             _ <- connectionType match {
174               case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client =>
175                 response.tryGet
176                   .map(_.isEmpty)
177                   .ifM(
178                     PseudoHeaders.headersToResponseNoBody(h) match {
179                       case Some(resp) =>
180                         val iResp = resp.withAttribute(H2Keys.StreamIdentifier, id)
181                         val outResp = resp.headers
182                           .get[org.http4s.headers.Trailer]
183                           .fold(iResp)(_ =>
184                             iResp.withAttribute(
185                               org.http4s.Message.Keys.TrailerHeaders[F],
186                               s.trailers.get.rethrow,
187                             )
188                           )
189                         response.complete(
190                           Either.right(outResp)
191                         ) >>
192                           resp.contentLength.traverse(length =>
193                             state.update(s => s.copy(contentLengthCheck = Some((length, 0))))
194                           ) >> {
195                             if (newstate == StreamState.Closed) onClosed else Applicative[F].unit
196                           }
197                       case None =>
198                         logger.error("Headers Unable to be parsed") >>
199                           rstStream(H2Error.ProtocolError)
200                     },
201                     s.trailers
202                       .complete(
203                         Either.right(
204                           org.http4s
205                             .Headers(h.toList.map(org.http4s.Header.ToRaw.keyValuesToRaw): _*)
206                         )
207                       )
208                       .void,
209                   )
210               case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server =>
211                 request.tryGet
212                   .map(_.isEmpty)
213                   .ifM(
214                     PseudoHeaders.headersToRequestNoBody(h) match {
215                       case Some(req) =>
216                         val iReq = req.withAttribute(H2Keys.StreamIdentifier, id)
217                         val outReq = req.headers
218                           .get[org.http4s.headers.Trailer]
219                           .fold(iReq)(_ =>
220                             iReq.withAttribute(
221                               org.http4s.Message.Keys.TrailerHeaders[F],
222                               s.trailers.get.rethrow,
223                             )
224                           )
225                         request.complete(
226                           Either.right(outReq)
227                         ) >>
228                           req.contentLength.traverse(length =>
229                             state.update(s => s.copy(contentLengthCheck = Some((length, 0))))
230                           ) >> {
231                             if (newstate == StreamState.Closed) onClosed else Applicative[F].unit
232                           }
233                       case None =>
234                         logger.error("Headers Unable to be parsed") >>
235                           rstStream(H2Error.ProtocolError)
236                     },
237                     s.trailers
238                       .complete(
239                         Either.right(
240                           org.http4s
241                             .Headers(h.toList.map(org.http4s.Header.ToRaw.keyValuesToRaw): _*)
242                         )
243                       )
244                       .void,
245                   )
246             }
247           } yield ()
248         case StreamState.HalfClosedRemote | StreamState.Closed =>
249           goAway(H2Error.StreamClosed)
250         case StreamState.ReservedLocal =>
251           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
252       }
253     }
254 
255   def receivePushPromise(
256       headers: H2Frame.PushPromise,
257       continuations: H2Frame.Continuation*
258   ): F[Unit] = state.get.flatMap { s =>
259     connectionType match {
260       case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client =>
261         s.state match {
262           case StreamState.Idle =>
263             val block = headers.headerBlock ++ continuations.foldLeft(ByteVector.empty) {
264               case (acc, cont) => acc ++ cont.headerBlockFragment
265             }
266             for {
267               h <- hpack.decodeHeaders(block).onError { case e =>
268                 logger.error(e)("Issue in headers"); goAway(H2Error.CompressionError)
269               }
270               _ <- state.update(s => s.copy(state = StreamState.ReservedRemote))
271               _ <- PseudoHeaders.headersToRequestNoBody(h) match {
272                 case Some(req) =>
273                   s.request
274                     .complete(
275                       Either.right(
276                         req
277                           .withAttribute(H2Keys.StreamIdentifier, id)
278                           .withAttribute(
279                             H2Keys.PushPromiseInitialStreamIdentifier,
280                             headers.identifier,
281                           )
282                       )
283                     )
284                     .void
285                 case None => rstStream(H2Error.ProtocolError)
286               }
287             } yield ()
288 
289           case _ => goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
290         }
291       case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server =>
292         goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
293     }
294   }
295 
296   def receiveData(data: H2Frame.Data): F[Unit] = state.get.flatMap { s =>
297     s.state match {
298       case StreamState.Open | StreamState.HalfClosedLocal =>
299         val newSize = s.readWindow - data.data.size.toInt
300         val newState = if (data.endStream) s.state match {
301           case StreamState.Open => StreamState.HalfClosedRemote
302           case StreamState.HalfClosedLocal => StreamState.Closed
303           case s => s
304         }
305         else s.state
306         val sizeReadOk = if (data.endStream) {
307           s.contentLengthCheck.forall { case (max, current) => max === (current + data.data.size) }
308         } else true
309 
310         val isClosed = newState == StreamState.Closed
311 
312         val needsWindowUpdate = newSize <= (localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize / 2)
313         for {
314           _ <- state.update(s =>
315             s.copy(
316               state = newState,
317               readWindow =
318                 if (needsWindowUpdate) localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize else newSize,
319               contentLengthCheck = s.contentLengthCheck.map { case (max, current) =>
320                 (max, current + data.data.size)
321               },
322             )
323           )
324           _ <-
325             if (sizeReadOk) s.readBuffer.offer(Either.right(data.data))
326             else rstStream(H2Error.ProtocolError)
327 
328           _ <-
329             if (needsWindowUpdate && !isClosed && sizeReadOk)
330               enqueue.offer(
331                 Chunk.singleton(
332                   H2Frame.WindowUpdate(id, localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize - newSize)
333                 )
334               )
335             else Applicative[F].unit
336           _ <- if (isClosed && sizeReadOk) onClosed else Applicative[F].unit
337         } yield ()
338       case StreamState.Idle =>
339         goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
340       case StreamState.HalfClosedRemote | StreamState.Closed =>
341         rstStream(H2Error.StreamClosed)
342       case StreamState.ReservedLocal | StreamState.ReservedRemote =>
343         goAway(H2Error.InternalError) // Not Implemented Push promise Support
344     }
345   }
346 
347   def rstStream(error: H2Error): F[Unit] = {
348     val rst = error.toRst(id)
349     for {
350       s <- state.modify(s => (s.copy(state = StreamState.Closed), s))
351       _ <- enqueue.offer(Chunk.singleton(rst))
352       t = new CancellationException(s"Sending RstStream, cancelling: $rst")
353       _ <- s.writeBlock.complete(Left(t))
354       _ <- s.request.complete(Left(t))
355       _ <- s.response.complete(Left(t))
356       _ <- s.readBuffer.offer(Left(t))
357       _ <- onClosed
358     } yield ()
359 
360   }
361 
362   // Broadcast Frame
363   // Will eventually allow us to know we can retry if we are above the processed window declared
364   def receiveGoAway(goAway: H2Frame.GoAway): F[Unit] = for {
365     s <- state.modify(s => (s.copy(state = StreamState.Closed), s))
366     t = new CancellationException(s"Received GoAway, cancelling: $goAway")
367     _ <- s.writeBlock.complete(Left(t))
368     _ <- s.request.complete(Left(t))
369     _ <- s.response.complete(Left(t))
370     _ <- s.readBuffer.offer(Left(t))
371     _ <- onClosed
372   } yield ()
373 
374   def receiveRstStream(rst: H2Frame.RstStream): F[Unit] = for {
375     s <- state.modify(s => (s.copy(state = StreamState.Closed), s))
376     t = new CancellationException(
377       s"Received RstStream, cancelling: $rst"
378     ) // Unsure of this, but also unsure about exposing custom throwable
379     _ <- s.writeBlock.complete(Left(t))
380     _ <- s.request.complete(Left(t))
381     _ <- s.response.complete(Left(t))
382     _ <- s.readBuffer.offer(Left(t))
383     _ <- onClosed
384   } yield ()
385 
386   // Important for telling folks we can send more data
387   def receiveWindowUpdate(window: H2Frame.WindowUpdate): F[Unit] = for {
388     newWriteBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
389     t <- state.modify { s =>
390       val oldSize = s.writeWindow
391       val newSize = oldSize + window.windowSizeIncrement
392       val sizeValid = (s.writeWindow >= 0 && newSize >= 0) || s.writeWindow < 0 // Less than 2^31-1
393       val newS = s.copy(writeBlock = newWriteBlock, writeWindow = newSize)
394       // println(s"Receive Window Update $newS - increment: ${window.windowSizeIncrement} oldSize: $oldSize")
395       (newS, (s.writeBlock, sizeValid))
396     }
397     (oldWriteBlock, valid) = t
398 
399     _ <- {
400       if (!valid) rstStream(H2Error.FlowControlError)
401       else oldWriteBlock.complete(Right(())).void
402     }
403   } yield ()
404 
405   def modifyWriteWindow(amount: Int): F[Unit] = for {
406     newWriteBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
407     oldWriteBlock <- state.modify { s =>
408       val newSize = s.writeWindow + amount
409       val newS = s.copy(writeBlock = newWriteBlock, writeWindow = newSize)
410       // println(s"Modify Write Window $newS")
411       (newS, s.writeBlock)
412     }
413 
414     _ <- oldWriteBlock.complete(Right(())).void
415   } yield ()
416 
417   def getRequest: F[org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure]] = state.get.flatMap(_.request.get.rethrow)
418   def getResponse: F[org.http4s.Response[fs2.Pure]] = state.get.flatMap(_.response.get.rethrow)
419 
420   def readBody: Stream[F, Byte] = {
421     def p: Pull[F, Byte, Unit] =
422       Pull.eval(state.get).flatMap { state =>
423         val closed =
424           state.state == StreamState.HalfClosedRemote || state.state == StreamState.Closed
425         if (closed) {
426           def p2: Pull[F, Byte, Unit] = Pull.eval(state.readBuffer.tryTake).flatMap {
427             case Some(Right(s)) => Pull.output(Chunk.byteVector(s)) >> p2
428             case Some(Left(e)) => Pull.raiseError(e)
429             case None => Pull.done
430           }
431           p2
432         } else {
433           def p2: Pull[F, Byte, Unit] = Pull.eval(state.readBuffer.tryTake).flatMap {
434             case Some(Right(s)) => Pull.output(Chunk.byteVector(s)) >> p2
435             case Some(Left(e)) => Pull.raiseError(e)
436             case None => p
437           }
438           Pull.eval(Concurrent[F].race(state.readBuffer.take, state.trailers.get)).flatMap {
439             case Left(Right(b)) => Pull.output(Chunk.byteVector(b))
440             case Left(Left(e)) => Pull.raiseError(e)
441             case Right(_) => Pull.done
442           } >> p2
443         }
444       }
445     p.stream
446   }
447 
448 }
449 
450 private[h2] object H2Stream {
451   final case class State[F[_]](
452       state: StreamState,
453       writeWindow: Int,
454       writeBlock: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]],
455       readWindow: Int,
456       request: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure]]],
457       response: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Response[fs2.Pure]]],
458       trailers: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Headers]],
459       readBuffer: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Either[Throwable, ByteVector]],
460       contentLengthCheck: Option[(Long, Long)],
461   ) {
462     override def toString: String =
463       s"H2Stream.State(state=$state, writeWindow=$writeWindow, readWindow=$readWindow, contentLengthCheck=$contentLengthCheck)"
464   }
465 
466   sealed trait StreamState
467   object StreamState {
468     /*
469                                   +--------+
470                           send PP |        | recv PP
471                         ,--------|  idle  |--------.
472                         /         |        |         \
473                       v          +--------+          v
474                 +----------+          |           +----------+
475                 |          |          | send H /  |          |
476         ,------| reserved |          | recv H    | reserved |------.
477         |      | (local)  |          |           | (remote) |      |
478         |      +----------+          v           +----------+      |
479         |          |             +--------+             |          |
480         |          |     recv ES |        | send ES     |          |
481         |   send H |     ,-------|  open  |-------.     | recv H   |
482         |          |    /        |        |        \    |          |
483         |          v   v         +--------+         v   v          |
484         |      +----------+          |           +----------+      |
485         |      |   half   |          |           |   half   |      |
486         |      |  closed  |          | send R /  |  closed  |      |
487         |      | (remote) |          | recv R    | (local)  |      |
488         |      +----------+          |           +----------+      |
489         |           |                |                 |           |
490         |           | send ES /      |       recv ES / |           |
491         |           | send R /       v        send R / |           |
492         |           | recv R     +--------+   recv R   |           |
493         | send R /  `----------->|        |<-----------'  send R / |
494         | recv R                 | closed |               recv R   |
495         `----------------------->|        |<----------------------'
496                                   +--------+
497 
498             send:   endpoint sends this frame
499             recv:   endpoint receives this frame
500 
501             H:  HEADERS frame (with implied CONTINUATIONs)
502             PP: PUSH_PROMISE frame (with implied CONTINUATIONs)
503             ES: END_STREAM flag
504             R:  RST_STREAM frame
505      */
506 
507     case object Idle extends StreamState // Transition to ReservedLocal/ReservedRemote/Open
508     case object ReservedLocal extends StreamState // Transition to HalfClosedRemote/Closed
509     case object ReservedRemote extends StreamState // Transition to HalfClosedLocal/Closed
510     case object Open extends StreamState // Transition to HalfClosedRemote/HalfClosedLocal/Closed
511     case object HalfClosedRemote extends StreamState // Transition to Closed
512     case object HalfClosedLocal extends StreamState // Transition to Closed
513     case object Closed extends StreamState // Terminal
514 
515   }
516 }
